    <a id="4067" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4485" class="Function">is-not-contractible-Fin</a><a id="4090" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4092" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7604" class="Function">succ-Fin</a><a id="4100" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="4102" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#4375" class="Function">is-contr-Fin-one-ℕ</a><a id="4120" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
## Idea

2-element types are types that are merely equivalent to the standard 2-element type `Fin 2`.

## Definition

### The condition that a type has two elements

<pre class="Agda"><a id="has-two-elements-Prop"></a><a id="4301" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4301" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4323" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4325" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4326" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4326" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4328" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4330" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4335" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4337" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4339" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4342" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4326" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4344" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4346" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1322" class="Function">UU-Prop</a> <a id="4354" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4326" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4356" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4301" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4378" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4378" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4380" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4382" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4278" class="Function">has-cardinality-Prop</a> <a id="4403" class="Number">2</a> <a id="4405" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4378" class="Bound">X</a>

<a id="has-two-elements"></a><a id="4408" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4408" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4425" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4427" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4428" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4428" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4430" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4432" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4437" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4439" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4441" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4444" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4428" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4446" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4448" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4451" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4428" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4453" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4408" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4470" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4470" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4472" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4474" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1424" class="Function">type-Prop</a> <a id="4484" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4485" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4301" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4507" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4470" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4508" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="is-prop-has-two-elements"></a><a id="4511" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4511" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4538" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4539" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4539" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4541" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4543" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4548" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4550" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4551" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4551" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4555" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4558" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4539" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4559" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4561" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4563" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1246" class="Function">is-prop</a> <a id="4571" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4572" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4408" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="4589" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4551" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4590" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4592" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4511" class="Function">is-prop-has-two-elements</a> <a id="4617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4618" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4618" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4619" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4621" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4622" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4622" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4623" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4625" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4627" href="foundation-core.propositions.html#1491" class="Function">is-prop-type-Prop</a> <a id="4645" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4646" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4301" class="Function">has-two-elements-Prop</a> <a id="4668" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4622" class="Bound">X</a><a id="4669" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The type of all 2-element types of universe level `l`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4743" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4758" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4760" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4761" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4761" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4763" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4765" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4770" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4772" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4774" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4777" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4778" href="Agda.Primitive.html#780" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="4783" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4761" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4784" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="4786" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4801" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4801" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4803" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4805" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4569" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="4818" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4801" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4820" class="Number">2</a>

<a id="type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4823" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4823" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4843" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4845" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4846" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4846" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4848" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4850" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4855" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4857" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4859" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4874" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4846" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4876" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4878" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="4881" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4846" class="Bound">l</a>
<a id="4883" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4823" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4903" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4905" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#592" class="Field">pr1</a>

<a id="has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="4910" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4910" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4947" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="4951" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4952" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4952" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="4954" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4956" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="4961" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4963" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4964" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4964" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="4966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4968" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="4983" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4952" class="Bound">l</a><a id="4984" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4986" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4988" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4408" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5005" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5006" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4823" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5026" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4964" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5027" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5029" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4910" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5066" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5068" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#604" class="Field">pr2</a>
</pre>
## Properties

### Any 2-element type is inhabited

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-inhabited-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="5137" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5137" class="Function">is-inhabited-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5165" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5169" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5170" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5170" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5172" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5174" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5179" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5181" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5182" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5182" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5184" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5186" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5201" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5170" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5202" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5204" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5206" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2012" class="Function">type-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5222" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5223" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4823" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5243" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5182" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5244" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="5246" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5137" class="Function">is-inhabited-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5274" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5274" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5276" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="5280" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#5581" class="Function">apply-universal-property-trunc-Prop</a>
    <a id="5320" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5322" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4910" class="Function">has-two-elements-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5359" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5274" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5360" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="5366" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5368" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2510" class="Function">trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5379" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5380" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4823" class="Function">type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5400" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5274" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5401" class="Symbol">))</a>
    <a id="5408" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5410" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="5412" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5412" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5414" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5416" href="foundation.propositional-truncations.html#2096" class="Function">unit-trunc-Prop</a> <a id="5432" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5433" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="5443" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5412" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="5445" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#7019" class="Function">zero-Fin</a><a id="5453" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Any 2-element type is a set

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-set-has-two-elements"></a><a id="5502" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5502" class="Function">is-set-has-two-elements</a> <a id="5526" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="5530" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5531" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5531" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5533" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5535" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5540" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5542" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5543" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5543" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5547" href="foundation-core.universe-levels.html#222" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="5550" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5531" class="Bound">l</a><a id="5551" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5553" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5555" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4408" class="Function">has-two-elements</a> <a id="5572" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5543" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5574" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5576" href="foundation-core.sets.html#1099" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="5583" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5543" class="Bound">X</a>
<a id="5585" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5502" class="Function">is-set-has-two-elements</a> <a id="5609" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5609" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="5611" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5613" href="univalent-combinatorics.equality-finite-types.html#2361" class="Function">is-set-has-cardinality</a> <a id="5636" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5609" class="Bound">H</a>

<a id="is-set-type-2-Element-Type"></a><a id="5639" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#5639" class="Function">is-set-type-2-Element-Type</a> <a id="5666" class="Symbol">:</a>

### Characterization the identifications of `Fin 2` with a 2-element type `X`

#### Evaluating an equivalence and an automorphism at `0 : Fin 2`

<pre class="Agda"><a id="ev-zero-equiv-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="7591" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#7591" class="Function">ev-zero-equiv-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="7615" class="Symbol">:</a>

          <a id="18852" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="18854" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#18541" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="18856" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#18594" class="Bound">X</a><a id="18857" class="Symbol">))</a>

### The swapping equivalence has no fixpoints

<pre class="Agda"><a id="23851" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="23858" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#23858" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="23862" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23863" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#23863" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="23865" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23867" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="23872" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23874" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23875" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#23875" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="23877" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23879" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#4743" class="Function">2-Element-Type</a> <a id="23894" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#23863" class="Bound">l</a><a id="23895" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Evaluating an automorphism at `0 : Fin 2` is a group homomorphism

<pre class="Agda"><a id="preserves-add-aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="26475" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#26475" class="Function">preserves-add-aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="26509" class="Symbol">:</a>

  <a id="26531" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#641" class="Datatype">Id</a> <a id="26534" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26536" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#7887" class="Function">aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="26556" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26557" href="elementary-number-theory.modular-arithmetic-standard-finite-types.html#6155" class="Function">add-Fin</a> <a id="26565" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#26514" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="26567" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#26516" class="Bound">b</a><a id="26568" class="Symbol">))</a>
     <a id="26576" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26578" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#7887" class="Function">aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="26598" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#26514" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="26600" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#7843" class="Function Operator">∘e</a> <a id="26603" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#7887" class="Function">aut-point-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="26623" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#26516" class="Bound">b</a><a id="26624" class="Symbol">)</a>

### Any Σ-type over `Fin 2` is a coproduct

<pre class="Agda"><a id="is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ"></a><a id="27092" href="univalent-combinatorics.2-element-types.html#27092" class="Function">is-coprod-Σ-Fin-two-ℕ</a> <a id="27114" class="Symbol">:</a>

### For any equivalence `e : Fin 2 ≃ X`, any element of `X` is either `e 0` or it is `e 1`.
